 mri_label2label --srcsubject fsaverage --srclabel /gpfs/projects/adapt_lab/shared/ADS/data/BIDS_data/derivatives/freesurfer/fsaverage/label/rh.BA1_exvivo.label --trgsubject sub-ADS1915_ses-wave3 --trglabel ./rh.BA1_exvivo.label --hemi rh --regmethod surface 


srclabel = /gpfs/projects/adapt_lab/shared/ADS/data/BIDS_data/derivatives/freesurfer/fsaverage/label/rh.BA1_exvivo.label
srcsubject = fsaverage
trgsubject = sub-ADS1915_ses-wave3
trglabel = ./rh.BA1_exvivo.label
regmethod = surface

srchemi = rh
trghemi = rh
trgsurface = white
srcsurfreg = sphere.reg
trgsurfreg = sphere.reg
usehash = 1
Use ProjAbs  = 0, 0
Use ProjFrac = 0, 0
DoPaint 0
